The entrance to the lobby of the hotel is very low-key, even giving people a feeling that this should not be the main entrance of the hotel, which gives people a feeling of "very narrow at first, and talented people". After entering the lobby, it is another scene. The design of the lobby is very distinctive. The concierge of the hotel is facing the door instead of the front desk. The concierge staff will ask the guests to scan the Beijing Healthbao and measure their body temperature, and they will also remind the guests not to exit the Beijing Healthbao interface for a while to check in.
The check-in at the front desk was very fast, it gave me the impression that it took no more than five minutes, and the staff were very friendly, because it was my first time checking in, so they gave me a clear introduction to the layout of my room. This is really too friendly for first-time hotel guests.
The hotel is close to the 798 Art District, and the overall artistic a**osphere is also very strong. If you like to take pictures, there are actually many places worth shooting. After checking in, you can see three works of art on the way to the room. The most eye-catching and my favorite one is a sculpture at the elevator entrance. It is really very designed, but I forgot to take a photoüòì
When I arrived at the room, I felt how necessary the front desk staff were to introduce the room. The overall design of the room is hidden, but according to their descriptions, I can easily find bathrobes, slippers, mobile phone charging cables and other items that I need or may use during the trip. The layout of the room is also very reasonable. Although the room I booked is only 40 square meters, there is a clear distinction between the living area and the functional area. I think it can fully meet the needs of some long-term residents.
The concept of environmental protection and low carbon is implemented in all aspects of the hotel, from the wooden room card to the six small pieces that are all packaged in environmental protection, and then to the packaging bags for biscuits, it is difficult to see plastic products. In addition, the texture of the razor with the wooden handle is very good. It is hard to believe that this is a disposable razor, but the wooden handle is a little slippery when it gets wet with water, but the flaws are not concealed.
The equipment in the gym is great, the number of stationary equipment is arguably the largest variety in a hotel I've seen, not just a few treadmills and a few dumbbells that are better than nothing.
There are many kinds of breakfast. I tried egg rolls. The chef's craftsmanship is great~
